<Rate>5<//Rate><review>NEW BEST BREAKFAST BURRITO PLACE!
My coworkers and I used to get our breakfast burrito fix at Rafas Mexican, which is inside the shell station on Del Paso (by Kohls). Their burritos were known in the office as the best breakfast burritos until today.  The throne has been passed on to El Burrito.  First of all, their menu is a bit more creative. I just ordered two Chile Verde Breakfast Burritos (one for me and one for my co-worker).
Tender, delicious, buttery, perfectly done, salty pork meat, eggs, guacamole, beans, potatoes, and enough cheese to choke a sumo wrestler. I couldn't (and shouldn't) even finish it in one sitting.
They have a salsa & chips bar inside the restaurant and I'll DEFINATELY be revisiting.  I've got to venture into the rest of their menu, if not solely for the deadly (and heavenly) experience I just had.<//review>< Pics>

<resp>None<//resp>< review>
I needed some professional pictures for a new corporate job and quickly found out that it is not as easy to find as you might think. I needed my head shots in digital format for the graphics department and in order to preserve them long term. Most photo stores do not supply the jpeg format, only printed photos.  Many of the independent photographers were interested in telling a story with their "art" or capturing the "essence" of a person. That is all fine but i really just needed a professional image, in jpeg format, from a professional photographer, in a real studio. I am so fortunate to have found Laurens Antoine Photography. The website has a simple form to fill out, i received a response within the hour. Laurens himself called me to say that they had a cancellation and were able to get me in the next day. The entire process was so easy from the first email to the final photos. The studio is in a nice area of downtown, and Laurens has 2 very nice female assistants that help you. It is a half block from the Police headquarters, so it is very safe to walk the short distance from wherever you park. The studio is set up for different types of shoots, from close up employment pictures, to fun modeling pictures. I am a happy and friendly person, but for some reason, as soon as i get in front of a camera, i freeze up and look super nervous. It really is the weirdest thing. Laurens was so friendly and understanding and after a little talking i started to feel comfortable and relax. Soon i was in front of the camera, still a little nervous and not sure how to smile. Laurens told me not to smile. We just talked and joked and through his magic, i ended up with some really natural and awesome pictures, and yes i got them in jpeg format. Do yourself a favor and don't bother looking anywhere else. I highly recommend Laurens Antoine Photography<//review>
